The text is a set of guidelines for creating a final terms document, specifically for an offer to the public of securities (such as shares or bonds). The guidelines cover various aspects of the offering, including:

1. **Investor categories**: The types of investors eligible for the offer.
2. **Plan of distribution and allotment**: Details on how the securities will be allocated to applicants.
3. **Pricing**: Information on the expected price of the securities, including any expenses or taxes charged to subscribers or purchasers.
4. **Placing and underwriting**: Details on the coordinators, paying agents, depository agents, underwriters, and placers involved in the offer.
5. **Admission to trading and dealing arrangements**: Information on whether the securities will be admitted to trading on specific markets, including any intermediaries for secondary trading.

Additionally, there are sections on:

* Guarantor information (if applicable)
* Annexes with additional information required by law or regulation

The guidelines aim to provide a comprehensive overview of the offer process and ensure that all necessary information is disclosed to investors.

The text appears to be a summary of technical requirements for radio equipment in the European Union, specifically related to the implementation of Directive 2014/53/EU on electrical and electronic equipment.

Key points include:

1. **DAA (Device Assignment Algorithm) mitigation technique**: Devices implementing DAA are permitted to operate with a maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of -41.3 dBm/MHz in specific frequency ranges, including the 3.1 GHz - 4.8 GHz and 8.5 GHz - 9 GHz bands.

2. **LBT (Listen Before Talk) mechanism**: Devices using LBT are permitted to operate with a maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of:
	* -70 dBm/MHz in the 1,215 GHz to 1,73 GHz frequency range
	* -50 dBm/MHz and -10 dBm/50 MHz in the 2,5 GHz to 2,69 GHz and 2,7 GHz to 3,4 GHz frequency ranges

3. **Radio Astronomy Service (RAS)**: The total power spectral density must be below -65 dBm/MHz in the 2,69 GHz to 2,7 GHz and 4,8 GHz to 5 GHz bands.

4. **Limitations on Duty Cycle**: Limitation of duty cycle to 10% per second.

5. **No fixed outdoor installations are permitted**.

6. **Alternative mitigation techniques**: Alternative mitigation techniques may be used if they ensure at least an equivalent performance and level of spectrum protection in order to comply with the corresponding essential requirements of Directive 2014/53/EU and respect the technical requirements of this Decision.

7. **Note 5 applies**: When DAA or LDC is implemented, note 5 applies.

The text is a summary of requirements for the European Union's Emissions Trading System (EU ETS). Here's the key information:

**General Requirements**

* The EU ETS system, also known as the Union Registry (EUTL), requires certain general information to be displayed on its public website.
* This includes national allocation tables, total allowances held in the Union Registry, fees charged by national administrators, and other relevant data.

**Monthly Reports**

* On 30 April each year, the EUTL must display specific information about completed transactions, including:
	+ Account holder name and account identifier
	+ Amount of allowances or Kyoto units involved
	+ Transaction identification code
	+ Date and time of completion (in Central European Time)
	+ Type of transaction
* Exemptions apply to certain transactions involving ETS management accounts.

**Real-time Information for Account Holders**

* The Union Registry's website must display real-time information to account holders, including:
	+ Current holdings of allowances and Kyoto units
	+ Proposed transactions initiated by the account holder
	+ List of completed transactions

**Additional Requirements**

* The system must track and report on various data points, such as allowance surrender and transfer transactions.
* The EUTL must display information about agreements in force pursuant to Article 25 of Directive 2003/87/EC.

Overall, the EU ETS requires a high degree of transparency and reporting from both the Union Registry and national administrators.

Here's a summary of the text:

**Article 26: Cross-reliance on audits**

* An audit based on internationally accepted standards providing reasonable assurance on financial statements and reports using Union contributions is considered the basis for overall assurance.
* The report and related documentation must be made available to the European Parliament, Commission, Court of Auditors, and Member State authorities.
* The auditor's independence and competence must be demonstrated.

**Article 27: Communication, knowledge sharing, and publicity**

* Project proponents must make publicly available information on their websites about projects supported by the Regulation, including a reference to Innovation Fund support received.
* Coherent, effective, and targeted information must be provided to multiple audiences, including media and the public.
* The Innovation Fund logo or promotional elements must be used in all communication and knowledge-sharing activities.
* Detailed information on planned actions is required for the knowledge-sharing plan submitted under Article 10(3).
* The implementing body will perform information, communication, and promotion actions relating to Innovation Fund support and results.

**Article 28: Entry into force**

* The Regulation enters into force on the 20th day following its publication in the Official Journal of the European Union.
* It is binding in its entirety and directly applicable in all Member States.

The text outlines the procedures for acceptance and validation of aircraft certificates issued by Competent Authorities in both the European Union (EU) and China. Here's a summary of the key points:

**General Principles**

* The process involves cooperation between EU and Chinese Competent Authorities to ensure compliance with international standards.
* Data and information exchange is facilitated through technical implementation procedures.

**Certificates Issued within the EU Regulatory System**

* Type certificates issued by the EU Competent Authority are validated in accordance with Level of Involvement principles.
* Some data, such as aircraft flight manuals, engine installation manuals, and weight balance manuals, will be automatically accepted.
* Supplemental type certificates and significant major changes require validation through an administrative process.
* Minor changes and repairs approved by the EU Competent Authority or an approved organization can be automatically accepted.

**Certificates Issued within the Chinese Regulatory System**

* Type certificates issued by the Chinese Technical Agent are validated in accordance with Level of Involvement principles.
* Supplemental type certificates, major changes, and Technical Standard Order Approvals require validation through an administrative process.
* Minor changes and repairs approved by the Chinese Competent Authority can be automatically accepted.

**Implementation Provisions**

* The administrative process involves no technical investigation when the complete application package is received.
* Validation times are typically within 3-5 weeks, depending on complexity.
* The classification of Supplemental type certificates and major changes as significant or non-significant is determined by the Certificating Authority based on design changes and revisions to certification specifications.

Overall, the text establishes procedures for cooperation between EU and Chinese Competent Authorities to ensure compliance with international standards, facilitate data exchange, and validate aircraft certificates.

* The exchange trailer specifies the interchange trailer and its purpose.

* Business rules specify conditions under which certain data elements must be completed.

Overall, this code list is an essential reference for shipping and port authorities, as well as other stakeholders involved in maritime transactions.

The LUC (Licensing and Certification) holder must provide a manual that describes its organization, procedures, and activities carried out. The manual should be amended as necessary to retain an up-to-date description of the organization and copies of amendments shall be provided to the competent authority.

Key processes for making personnel aware of their responsibilities and procedure for amending this documentation include:

* Safety reporting and internal investigations
* Operational control
* Communication on safety
* Training and safety promotion
* Compliance monitoring
* Safety risk management
* Management of change
* Interface between organizations
* Use of subcontractors and partners

An independent function should be included to monitor the compliance and adequacy of the fulfillment of relevant requirements, including a system to provide feedback to the accountable manager.

The UAS operator's safety management system may be integrated with additional organization certificates within the scope of Regulation (EU) No 2018/1139.

When issuing an LUC, the competent authority must:

* Specify terms and conditions of the privilege granted
* Grant the privilege without submitting operational declarations or applying for authorizations

Changes in the LUC management system require prior approval from the competent authority. The LUC is not transferable except for changes to ownership approved by the competent authority.

The duration and validity of an LUC are unlimited, subject to continuous compliance with relevant requirements and non-surrender or revocation.

UAS operators must grant access to facilities, UAS, documents, records, data, procedures, or materials relevant to their activity to authorized persons for demonstrating compliance.

The provided text appears to be a partial excerpt from an EU regulation related to Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAS). Here's a summary of the key points:

**Simplified Declaration of Conformity**

* The simplified EU declaration of conformity is required for UAS that are classified as Class 1, 2, or 3.
* The declaration includes information on the sound power level and compliance with relevant regulations.

**Noise Test Code**

* This Part outlines the methods for measuring airborne noise and determining the A-weighted sound power levels of UAS.
* The test code specifies the basic noise emission standard (EN ISO 3744:2010) and detailed requirements for testing, including:
	+ Installation and mounting conditions
	+ Operating conditions during test
	+ Calculation of surface time-averaged sound pressure level

**Indication of Guaranteed Sound Power Level**

* The indication must consist of a single number representing the guaranteed sound power level in dB, followed by an "LWA" symbol, and accompanied by a pictogram.

**Maximum Sound Power Level per Class of UAS**

* The maximum sound power levels are specified for each class of UAS:
	+ Class C1: 85 dB (as from entry into force), 83 dB (2 years after entry into force), and 81 dB (4 years after entry into force).
	+ Class C2: 90 dB (as from entry into force), 88 dB (2 years after entry into force), and 86 dB (4 years after entry into force).

Here's a summary of the text:

**Verification Procedure for Market Surveillance**

* The verification tolerances in Table 12 relate only to Member State authorities and not to suppliers as an allowed tolerance.
* If a model detects its own test conditions, it shall be considered non-compliant.
* When verifying compliance, Member State authorities shall apply the following procedure:
	1. Verify one single unit of the model.
	2. Check if values given in technical documentation are not more favorable for supplier than corresponding values in test reports and energy efficiency class on label.
	3. If results in points 2(a) and (b) are achieved, check if determined values comply with verification tolerances as listed in Table 12.
	4. If not, select three additional units of same model for testing (or one or more equivalent models).
	5. Check if arithmetic mean of determined values complies with verification tolerances.
* The Member State authorities shall use the measurement and calculation methods set out in Annex IV.
* No other tolerances (e.g., from harmonized standards) shall be applied.

**Verification Tolerances**

| Parameters | Verification Tolerances |
| --- | --- |
| Net Volume and Gross Volume | ±3% or 1 L lower, whichever is greater |
| Total Diel (TDA) and Compartment TDA | ±3% lower |
| Energetic Daily (Edaily) | ±10% higher |
| Active Energy (AE) | ±10% higher |

###################################################
This Regulation sets standards for light sources, including LED and OLED products. Here are the key points:

**Light Source Requirements**

* The light source shall meet certain technical requirements, such as:
	+ Luminous flux of at least 25 lm/W
	+ Colour rendering index (CRI) of at least 80
	+ Chromaticity coordinates within specific ranges
	+ Colour temperature within a specific range
* Light sources with linear geometry are considered scalable if they can be mounted to a length of 50 cm or more

**Verification Testing**

* Market surveillance authorities shall verify the product's compliance with these requirements by testing a sample of 10 units
* The test methods include:
	+ Measuring luminous flux, luminous flux density, and colour rendering index
	+ Verifying that light sources can be controlled to adjust color temperature and beam angle
	+ Testing for survival factor and lumen maintenance

**Endurance Testing**

* LED and OLED light sources shall undergo endurance testing to verify their lumen maintenance and survival factor
* The test consists of 1,200 cycles of repeated switching on and off without interruption
* Units that fail the test are removed from consideration as a light source

**Environmental Aspects**

* The best available technology for light sources in terms of efficacy is:
	+ Mains voltage non-directional light sources: 120-140 lm/W
	+ Mains voltage directional light sources: 90-100 lm/W
	+ Directional light sources not operating on the mains: 85-95 lm/W
* The best available technology for separate control gears has an energy efficiency of 95%

**Mercury Content**

* There is no mercury content in light sources with this Regulation.

Note: This summary focuses on the key points and requirements outlined in the text.

Der Text beschreibt Anforderungen und Empfehlungen für eine Emissionsvermittlung in der EU. Hier sind die wichtigsten Punkte:

1.  **Veröffentlichung von Prospekten:** Die Emission muss mit einem Prospekt belegt werden, der alle relevanten Informationen enthält, um den Anlegern ein fundiertes Urteil zu ermöglichen.
2.  **Anzeige der Plattform:** Die Emittentin muss die Plattform angemeldet haben und die Plattform soll mindestens zwei Tage vor der ersten Veröffentlichung von Wertpapieren der Emission offiziell bestätigen, dass es sich um eine Emissionsvermittlung handelt.
3.  **Zulassung zum Handel:** Die Emittentin muss die Wertpapiere auf allen relevanten Märkten zulassen oder beantragen, in denen sie öffentlich angeboten werden.
4.  **Festlegungen für komplexe derivative Wertpapiere**: Es sollen Beispiele für komplexe derivative Wertpapiere gegeben werden, um die Anleger über die Risiken und Chancen der Emission aufzuklären.
5.  **Seriennummer:** Die Seriennummer muss bei jeder Zertifikatsvergabe oder Übernahme von Obligationen angegeben werden.

Es gibt verschiedene Kategorien für Emittenten, in denen spezielle Anforderungen gelten, wie z.B. für Immobilien- oder Bergbaugesellschaften, Investmentgesellschaften oder Start-up-Unternehmen.
###################################################
Es gibt verschiedene Vorschriften und Anforderungen für Funkanlagen, um die Interferenzen und Störungen zu minimieren:

1.  **Frequenzschutz**: Funkanlagen müssen bestimmte Frequenzbänder nicht stören, z.B. der Radioastronomiefunkdienst (RAS) 2,69-2,7 GHz und 4,8-5 GHz.
2.  **Leistungsdichte**: Funkanlagen müssen eine bestimmte Leistungsdichte nicht überschreiten, um Störungen zu minimieren: *   In den Frequenzbereichen 2,5-2,69 GHz und 4,8-5 GHz muss die insgesamt abgestrahlte spektrale Leistungsdichte 10 dB unter der maximalen spektralen Leistungsdichte (EIRP) liegen. *   Im Frequenzbereich 3,4-3,8 GHz muss die insgesamt abgestrahlte spektrale Leistungsdichte 5 dB unter der maximalen spektralen Leistungsdichte (EIRP) liegen.
3.  **Sendezeitanteil**: Funkanlagen dürfen nicht mehr als 10 % des gesamten Zeitintervalls für Sendezeiten aufweisen.
4.  **Ortsfeste Anlagen**: Ortsfeste Anlagen sind nicht zugelassen.
5.  **LDC-Störungsminderungstechnik**: Innerhalb des Frequenzbands 3,1 GHz-4,8 GHz dürfen Geräte mit LDC-Störungsminderungstechnik betrieben werden. Die Störungsminderungstechnik zur Begrenzung des Sendezeitanteils (Low-Duty-Cycle, LDC) und ihre Grenzwerte sind in den Abschnitten 4.5.3.1, 4.5.3.2 und 4.5.3.3 der ETSI-Norm EN 302 065-1 V2.1.1 definiert.
6.  **DAA-Störungsminderungstechnik**: Innerhalb der Frequenzbänder 3,1 GHz-4,8 GHz und 8,5 GHz dürfen Geräte mit DAA-Störungsminderungstechnik betrieben werden. Die Störungsminderungstechnik zur Feststellung und Vermeidung benutzter Frequenzen (Detect-And-Avoid, DAA) und ihre Grenzwerte sind in den Abschnitten 4.5.1.1, 4.5.1.2 und 4.5.1.3 der ETSI-Norm EN 302 065-1 V2.1.1 definiert.
7.  **Technische Anforderungen**: Alternative Störungsminderungstechniken können angewandt werden, wenn sie ein mindestens gleichwertiges Leistungs- und Frequenzschutzniveau bieten, sodass die entsprechenden wesentlichen Anforderungen der Richtlinie 2014/53/EU und die technischen Anforderungen dieses Beschlusses erfüllt sind.

Einige der wichtigsten Punkte, die im Anhang zum EU-Emittierungshandelsrecht (EUTL) festgelegt sind:

1.  **Verwaltung von Zertifikaten und Kyoto-Einheiten**: Der EUTL verantwortet die Verwaltung aller registrierten Zertifikate und Einheiten, einschließlich der Übertragung und des Ausstellens von Transaktionskennungen.
2.  **Transaktionsregisterverzeichnis**: Das Unionsregister führt ein Transaktionsverzeichnis, in dem alle abgeschlossenen Transaktionen aufgezeichnet werden, einschließlich der beteiligten Konten, Zertifikate und Einheiten.
3.  **Kontoinhabern zugängliche Informationen**: Der Kontoinhaber kann die im Anhang genannten Informationen über seine Zertifikate und Einheiten sehen.
4.  **Abkommen und Zertifikate**: Der EUTL veröffentlicht jährlich eine Liste der im verbundenen Emissionshandelssystem verwendeten Zertifikate, einschließlich ihrer Zahl und des Guthabens an den verbundenen Markt.
5.  **Aktuelle Informationen**: Der Kontoinhaber kann die aktuelle Anzahl der übertragenen Zertifikate und Einheiten sowie eine Liste der vorgeschlagenen Transaktionen sehen.

Diese Informationen sind wichtig für die Aufrechterhaltung einer effizienten und transparenten Emissionshandelsverwaltung.

Es gibt verschiedene Vorgehensweisen zum Nachweis der Einhaltung von Vorschriften für ein Produkt, die in verschiedenen Bereichen unterschiedlich sind:

**Verwaltungstechnische Vorgehensweise**

*   **Erhebliche Änderungen und Reparaturen**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde genehmigt diese Änderungen.
*   **Nichtsignifikante erhebliche Änderungen und erhebliche Reparaturen**: Die Verwaltungstechnische Vorgehensweise wird automatisch angenommen. 
*   **Geringfügige Änderungen und Reparaturen, die von der Zertifizierungsbehörde genehmigt wurden**: Automatische Akzeptanz.

**Chinesisches Regulierungssystem**

*   **Musterzulassung**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde genehmigt diese Musterzulassung.
*   **Ergänzende Musterzulassung**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde genehmigt diese ergänzende Musterzulassung.
*   **TSO (Technische Beschreibung und Festlegungen)**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde genehmigt diese TSO (technischen Beschreibungen und Festlegungen).
*   **Geringfügige Änderungen und Reparaturen**: Automatische Akzeptanz.

**Durchführungsbestimmungen**

*   **Validierung**: Das vollständige Anwendungspaket wird an die Validierungsbehörde eingereicht.
*   **Einstufung in Kategorien (signifikant / nichtsignifikant)**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde entscheidet, ob eine Änderung signifikant oder nichtsignifikant ist. 
*   **Automatische Akzeptanz**: Bei einer Änderung, die bestimmte Kriterien erfüllt.
*   **Festlegung der Kategorisierung (Erheblichkeit / geringfügigkeit)**: Die Zertifizierungsbehörde betrachtet die Änderung im Kontext aller vorhergehenden einschlägigen Konstruktionsänderungen und der entsprechenden Änderungen der geltenden Zertifizierungsspezifikationen. 
*   **Genehmigungen von TSO (Technische Beschreibung und Festlegungen)**: Einige Genehmigungen werden im Rahmen eines gestrafften Validierungsprozesses validiert, der sich auf das technische Vertrautmachen ohne die Einbeziehung der Zertifizierungsbehörde beschränkt.
*   **Genehmigung von Änderungen**: Die Änderung ist automatisch signifikant.

Es gibt eine Reihe von Regeln und Anforderungen für UAS-Betriebe, die in einem LUC-Handbuch festgelegt sind. Hier sind die wichtigsten Punkte:

**LUC-Handbuch**

* Das LUC-Handbuch enthält Informationen über den UAS-Betreiber, seine Rechte, die genehmigten Betriebsarten und Bereiche, Gebiete oder Luftraumklassen.
* Es gibt eine Beschreibung des Sicherheitsmanagementsystems.

**Ausstellung eines LUC**

* Die zuständige Behörde stellt ein LUC aus, wenn der UAS-Betreiber die Bedingungen erfüllt (UAS.LUC.020, UAS.LUC.030 und UAS.LUC.040).
* Das LUC enthält die Identifizierung des UAS-Betreibers, seine Rechte und die genehmigten Betriebsarten.

**Rechte des LUC-Inhabers**

* Der LUC-Inhaber hat das Recht, seinen eigenen Betrieb zu genehmigen, ohne dass eine Betriebserklärung vorgelegt oder ein Antrag auf Betriebsgenehmigung gestellt werden muss.
* Es gibt besondere Beschränkungen oder Bedingungen.

**Änderungen des LUC-Managementsystems**

* Jede Änderung der Genehmigungsbedingungen oder das Sicherheitsmanagementsystem erfordert eine vorherige Genehmigung durch die zuständige Behörde.
* Änderungen an sich selbst ergeben keinen Grund zur Erneuerung eines LUC.

**Übertragbarkeit eines LUC**

* Ein LUC ist nicht übertragbar, es sei denn, es wurde von der zuständigen Behörde genehmigt, dass ein Wechsel des Eigentümers stattfindet.
* Die Genehmigung muss schriftlich erteilt werden.

**Gültigkeitsdauer eines LUC**

* Ein LUC ist für eine unbegrenzte Dauer gültig, solange der UAS-Betreiber die Anforderungen erfüllt und das LUC nicht zurückgegeben oder widerrufen wird.
* Bei Widerruf oder Rückgabe muss der UAS-Betreiber dies unverzüglich und digital bestätigen.

**Zugang**

* Der UAS-Betreiber hat jeder Person, die von der zuständigen Behörde hierfür ordnungsgemäß ermächtigt wurde, Zugang zu allen Anlagen, UAS, Unterlagen, Aufzeichnungen, Daten und Verfahren oder zum relevanten Material.
###################################################
Der Text beschreibt Standards für das Messen von Schallpegeln bei U-Bahnen, insbesondere für die Geräuschmessung der U-Bahn-Untergrundanlagen (UA). Die Standards sind enthalten in EN ISO 3744:2010.

Zu den wichtigen Informationen gehören:

*   Die Messfläche muss eine halbkugelförmige Oberfläche gemäß Nummer 7.2.3 der EN ISO 3744:2010 umhüllt sein.
*   Der Ursprung der Messfläche liegt im Punkt O auf der Grundebene direkt unter dem UA.
*   Die Geräuschmessungen müssen bei MTOM (maximaler Trockenmasse) und mit einer vollständig geladenen Batterie des UA durchgeführt werden.
*   Das UA muss 0,5 m über der reflektierenden Ebene schweben.
*   Der A-bewertete zeitlich gemittelte Oberflächen-Schalldruckpegel ist für jede UA-Konfiguration mindestens dreimal zu bestimmen.
*   Weichen mindestens zwei der bestimmten Werte um nicht mehr als 1 dB voneinander ab, sind keine weiteren Messungen notwendig.
*   Der zur Berechnung des Schallleistungspegels einer UA-Konfiguration zu verwendende zeitlich gemittelte Oberflächen-Schalldruckpegel ist das arithmetische Mittel der beiden höchsten Werte, die um nicht mehr als 1 dB voneinander abweichen.
*   In den Bericht sind die zur Identifizierung der geprüften Geräuschquelle notwendigen technischen Daten sowie die Prüfvorschrift und die Akustik-Daten anzugeben.

Darüber hinaus enthalten die Standards folgende Kennzeichnungen:

*   Die Kennzeichnung des garantierten Schallleistungspegels muss aus dem Zahlenwert des garantierten Schallleistungspegels in dB, dem Zeichen LWA und einem Piktogramm bestehen.
*   Bei Verkleinerung der Kennzeichnung je nach Größe des Geräts müssen die sich aus der obigen Zeichnung ergebenden Proportionen eingehalten werden.
*   Die Höhe der Kennzeichnung sollte jedoch, soweit möglich, mindestens 20 mm betragen.

Darüber hinaus sind für jede UA-Klasse (C1 und C2) folgende Maximalwerte festgelegt:

|   UA-Klasse |   MTOM m in Gramm |   Maximaler Schallleistungspegel LWA in dB |
|  :--: |  :-----------------: |  :------------------------: |
|   C1   | 250 ≤ m < 900     | 85                           |
|   C2   | 900 ≤ m < 4 000    | 85                           |

Die wichtigsten Informationen können wie folgt zusammengefasst werden:

*   Die Messfläche muss eine halbkugelförmige Oberfläche umhüllen.
*   Der Ursprung der Messfläche liegt im Punkt O auf der Grundebene direkt unter dem UA.
*   Die Geräuschmessungen müssen bei MTOM und mit einer vollständig geladenen Batterie durchgeführt werden.
*   Das UA muss 0,5 m über der reflektierenden Ebene schweben.
*   Der A-bewertete zeitlich gemittelte Oberflächen-Schalldruckpegel ist für jede UA-Konfiguration mindestens dreimal zu bestimmen.
*   Weichen mindestens zwei der bestimmten Werte um nicht mehr als 1 dB voneinander ab, sind keine weiteren Messungen notwendig.
*   Der zur Berechnung des Schallleistungspegels einer UA-Konfiguration zu verwendende zeitlich gemittelte Oberflächen-Schalldruckpegel ist das arithmetische Mittel der beiden höchsten Werte, die um nicht mehr als 1 dB voneinander abweichen.
*   In den Bericht sind die zur Identifizierung der geprüften Geräuschquelle notwendigen technischen Daten sowie die Prüfvorschrift und die Akustik-Daten anzugeben.
###################################################
Die Vorschrift beschreibt die Anforderungen für das Modell in Bezug auf den Nettorauminhalt, Bruttorauminhalt, Warenpräsentationsfläche und Edaily.

Es werden folgende Anforderungen genannt:

*   Der ermittelte Wert darf den angegebenen Wert um nicht mehr als 3 % oder 1 l unterschreiten.
*   Der ermittelte Wert darf den angegebenen Wert um nicht mehr als 10 % überschreiten.
*   Die Prüftoleranzen für die verschiedenen Parameter sind in Tabelle 12 aufgeführt.

Die Anforderungen müssen erfüllt sein, um das Modell als gleichwertig anzuerkennen.
###################################################
Der obige Text beschreibt die Prüfverfahren und Referenzwerte für LED- und OLED-Lichtquellen nach der EU-Verordnung über Energieeffizienz in Bezug auf Licht. Hier sind die wichtigsten Punkte zusammengefasst:

**Prüfung von LED- und OLED-Lichtquellen:**

1. Umgebungsbedingungen: Die Prüfung findet in einem Raum mit einer Temperatur von 25 °C und einer Luftgeschwindigkeit von weniger als 0,2 m/s statt.
2. Schaltzyklen: Die Lichtquelle wird über 1 200 kontinuierlich wiederholte Schaltzyklen betrieben.
3. Messung des anfänglichen und abschließenden Lichtstroms: Der anfängliche Lichtstrom wird vor dem Schaltzyklus gemessen, und der abschließende Lichtstrom wird nach dem Schaltzyklus gemessen.
4. Berechnung des ermittelten Wertes des Lichtstromerhalts XLMF %: Der am Ende der Prüfung gemessene Lichtstrom wird durch den anfänglichen Lichtstrom dividiert, und die Ergebnisse werden über alle Exemplare, die nicht ausgefallen sind, gemittelt.

**Referenzwerte:**

1. Netzspannungslichtquellen mit ungebündeltem Licht: 120-140 lm/W
2. Netzspannungslichtquellen mit gebündeltem Licht: 90-100 lm/W
3. nicht direkt an die Netzspannung angeschlossene Lichtquellen mit gebündeltem Licht: 85-95 lm/W
4. stabförmige Lichtquellen (Röhren): 140-160 lm/W
5. separate Betriebsgeräte: Wirkungsgrad von 95 %

**Weitere Informationen:**

1. Die beste auf dem Markt verfügbare Technik für Lichtquellen enthält kein Quecksilber.
2. Produkte für bestimmte Anwendungen müssen bestimmte Merkmale aufweisen, was zu einer Abweichung von den Referenzwerten führen kann.

Diese Informationen sind wichtig, um die Energieeffizienz und Sicherheit von LED- und OLED-Lichtquellen zu bewerten.

Voici un résumé du texte :

**Exigences techniques pour les installations mobiles**

* Les installations mobiles doivent satisfaire aux exigences de puissance rayonnée totale dans les bandes de fréquences suivantes :
	+ 2,5 GHz à 2,69 GHz : densité spectrale de puissance totale inférieure de 10 dB à la densité spectrale de p.i.r.e. maximale
	+ 3,4 GHz à 3,8 GHz : densité spectrale de puissance totale inférieure de 5 dB à la densité spectrale de p.i.r.e. maximale
* La bande de 2,69 GHz à 2,7 GHz et de 4,8 GHz à 5 GHz utilisées par le service de radioastronomie (RAS) doivent avoir une densité spectrale de puissance totale inférieure à – 65 dBm/MHz.
* La limitation du temps de cycle est fixée à 10 % par seconde.

**Méthodes d'atténuation**

* Les méthodes LBT, LDC et DAA sont autorisées dans les bandes de 3,1 GHz à 4,8 GHz, avec des limites de puissance rayonnée totale :
	+ LDC : densité spectrale de p.i.r.e. moyenne maximale de – 41,3 dBm/MHz et une p.i.r.e de crête maximale de 0 dBm dans une largeur de bande de 50 MHz.
	+ DAA : densité spectrale de p.i.r.e. moyenne maximale de – 41,3 dBm/MHz et une p.i.r.e de crête maximale de 0 dBm dans une largeur de bande de 50 MHz.

**Exigences générales**

* Les installations mobiles doivent satisfaire aux exigences essentielles correspondantes de la directive 2014/53/UE.
* Des méthodes d'atténuation de substitution peuvent être utilisées si elles garantissent au moins une performance et un niveau de protection des radiofréquences équivalents.

**Note importante**

* En cas d'utilisation de la LDC ou de la DAA, la note 5 s'applique.

**Réglementation européenne du carbone**

L'article 24 de la directive 2003/87/CE établit le registre de l'Union, qui est chargé de gérer le système de droits d'émission lié. Le registre doit publier certaines informations sur son site web public.

**Informations publiées par le registre**

Le registre doit publier les informations suivantes :

* Les avoirs en quotas délivrés dans le système de droits d'émission lié qui sont détenus sur tous les comptes du registre de l'Union.
* Le nombre de quotas délivrés dans le système de droits d'émission lié qui sont utilisés à des fins de conformité dans le cadre du SEQE de l'Union européenne.
* La somme des quotas délivrés dans le système de droits d'émission lié qui ont été transférés sur des comptes du registre de l'Union au cours de l'année civile précédente.
* La somme des quotas qui ont été transférés sur des comptes du système de droits d'émission lié au cours de l'année civile précédente.

**Informations publiées par le EUTL**

Le EUTL doit publier les informations suivantes :

* Les transactions de transfert de quotas et d'unités de Kyoto réalisées au cours de l'année civile précédente, y compris le code pays.
* Le pourcentage (en nombre et en volume) des transactions de transfert de quotas et d'unités de Kyoto réalisées entre des comptes gérés par des États membres différents.

**Informations accessibles aux titulaires de compte**

Le registre de l'Union publie sur la partie de son site web réservée aux seuls titulaires de compte les informations suivantes :

* Les avoirs en quotas et en unités de Kyoto, y compris le code pays et, s'il y a lieu, l'indication de la période de dix ans au cours de laquelle les quotas ont été créés.
* La liste des transactions proposées par le titulaire de compte, précisant les éléments suivants : nom du titulaire du compte, code d'identification du compte source du transfert, nom du titulaire du compte et le code d'identification du compte destinataire, quantité de quotas ou d'unités de Kyoto concernées par la transaction, date et heure auxquelles la transaction a été réalisée.

Le texte décrit les procédures de validation et d'acceptation de certificats de type pour des produits, notamment dans le contexte de la certification chinoise et européenne. Voici un résumé des principales informations :

**Certificats de type**

* Certificat de type : acceptation automatique
* Certificat de type supplémentaire important : validation selon les principes du niveau de participation visés au point 4.4.2 de l’annexe et les procédures de mise en œuvre technique.
* Certificat de type non important : validation par un processus administratif figurant dans les procédures de mise en œuvre technique.

**Modifications et réparations**

* Modifications et réparations majeures approuvées par l'autorité compétente : acceptation automatique
* Agrément selon les spécifications techniques délivré par l'autorité compétente : validation selon les principes du niveau de participation visés au point 4.4.2 de l'annexe et les procédures de mise en œuvre technique.
* Modifications et réparations mineures approuvées par l'autorité compétente : acceptation automatique

**Certificats délivrés dans le cadre du système réglementaire chinois**

* Certificat de type délivré par l'agent technique chinois : validation selon les principes du niveau de participation visés au point 4.4.2 de l'annexe et les procédures de mise en œuvre technique.
* Agrément selon les spécifications techniques délivré par l'autorité compétente chinoise : validation selon les principes du niveau de participation visés au point 4.4.2 de l'annexe et les procédures de mise en œuvre technique.

**Dispositions d'application**

* Le processus administratif ne comporte aucune enquête technique.
* Les classifications mineures/majeures et importantes/non importantes sont établies par l'autorité de certification en fonction des critères et définitions énoncés dans la présente annexe.
* Pour déterminer si un certificat de type supplémentaire spécifique ou une modification majeure spécifique est important(e) ou non, l'autorité de certification examine la modification au regard de toutes les modifications de conception antérieures pertinentes ainsi que de toutes les révisions connexes des spécifications de certification applicables intégrées dans le certificat de type du produit. Sont considérées comme importantes les modifications qui répondent à l’un des critères suivants:
a) la configuration générale ou les principes de construction ne sont pas conservés;
b) les hypothèses retenues pour la certification du produit à modifier ne sont plus valables.

**Nature de la cargaison et classification code**

* Le code de classification de la cargaison est codé sur 16 positions
* Les codes sont :
	+ «5» : Autres, sans conteneur
	+ «6» : Véhicules
	+ «7» : RoRo
	+ «8» : Sur palettes
	+ «9» : En conteneurs
	+ «10» : Marchandises diverses en vrac
	+ «11» : Marchandises dangereuses
	+ «12» : Marchandises diverses
	+ «13» : Marchandises liquides
	+ «14» : Marchandises à température contrôlée
	+ «15» : Polluant environnemental
	+ «16» : Marchandises non dangereuses
	+ «17» : Diplomatique
	+ «18» : Militaire
	+ «19» : Produits nocifs
	+ «21» : Produits ménagers
	+ «22» : Marchandise surgelée
	+ «30» : Marchandise en vrac (sable, graviers, minerai, etc.)

**Mesures et attributs**

* La mesure de poids brut est codée sur 3 positions
* Les mesures sont significatives si elles concernent la quantité ou le poids de la cargaison
* Le code d'identification des mesures est codé sur 17 positions

**Messagerie et contrôle**

* La message est composée de deux parties : le trailer de message et l'intéchange
* Le trailer de message contient :
	+ Le nombre de segments dans un message
	+ Le numéro de référence du message
	+ L'interchange control count (1 si le code est XXXXX)
	+ L'interchange control reference (14 premières positions du numéro de référence du message)

**Règles opérationnelles**

* Si le code est XXXXX, cet élément de données doit être renseigné
* Les règles opérationnelles sont liées au recueil de l'OMI, à la directive 2010/65/UE et au code ISPS.

Ces informations fournissent un aperçu général des formats de message et de codes utilisés dans le domaine du transport maritime.

Voici un résumé des principaux points :

**Règlement du LUC**

* Le règlement du LUC (Licence d'Exploitation de l'Union Aérienne de Safran) est une attestation délivrée par l'autorité compétente après vérification que l'exploitant d'un UAS (Unité d'Exploration et de Sauvegarde Aéroportuaires) respecte les exigences du présent règlement.
* Le LUC contient des informations sur l'identité de l'exploitant, ses privilèges, le type d'exploitation autorisée, la zone ou la classe d'espace aérien autorisée et toute limite ou condition particulière.

**Privilèges du titulaire d'un LUC**

* L'autorité compétente précise les termes et conditions du privilège accordé à l'exploitant dans le LUC.
* Selon les conditions d'agrément, le titulaire d'un LUC est autorisé à exercer ses propres exploitations en exemptant son entreprise de la nécessité de soumettre une déclaration d'exploitation ou de demander une autorisation d'exploitation.

**Modifications du système de gestion du LUC**

* Toute modification importante apportée aux éléments du système de gestion de la sécurité du titulaire du LUC doit être approbée par l'autorité compétente.
* Les modifications doivent être effectuées avec préavis et suivies d'une mise à jour du manuel LUC.

**Transférabilité d'un LUC**

* Un LUC n'est pas transférable sauf en cas de changement de propriété de l'organisme, approuvé par l'autorité compétente.

**Durée et validité d'un LUC**

* Un LUC est délivré pour une durée illimitée. Il reste valide si le titulaire du LUC respecte les exigences applicables du présent règlement et de l'État membre qui a délivré le certificat.
* La restitution ou le retrait d'un LUC doit être effectué avec préavis et accompagné d'un accusé de réception sous forme numérique.

**Accès**

* Le titulaire d'un LUC permet à toute personne dûment autorisée par l'autorité compétente d'accéder à tout UAS, installation, document, registre, donnée, procédure ou matériel se rapportant à son activité.

Voici un résumé des textes :

**Norme EN ISO 3744 : 2010**

La norme standardise la conception et la mise en œuvre de sources sonores pour tests d'absorption acoustique.

**Objectif de la norme**

L'objectif de la norme est de définir les exigences techniques pour les sources sonores utilisées dans les essais d'absorption acoustique, afin de garantir des résultats précis et fiables.

**Exigences générales**

Les sources sonores doivent être conçues pour fonctionner correctement dans une large gamme de conditions environnementales et de charges de poussée.

**Conception de la source sonore**

La source sonore doit être plane, symétrique et uniforme. Elle doit également être capable de produire un signal acoustique uniforme sur tout le surface de mesurage.

**Montage de la source sonore**

L'UA (Unité d'essai) plane est montée à 0,5 m au-dessus du plan réfléchissant. La configuration de l'UA (hélices, accessoires, paramètres) est celle de l'UA tel que mis sur le marché.

**Surface de mesurage acoustique et ensemble de microphones**

L'UA est entièrement compris dans la surface de mesurage hémisphérique. Le nombre et le positionnement des microphones sont définis à l'annexe F de la norme EN ISO 3744:2010.

**Conditions de fonctionnement pendant l'essai**

Les essais acoustiques doivent être effectués lorsque l'UA vole en position stable, latéralement et verticalement, à 0,5 m au-dessus de l'origine de l'hémisphère de mesurage. La batterie de l'UA doit être complètement chargée.

**Calcul du niveau de pression acoustique surfacique moyenné**

Le niveau de pression acoustique surfacique moyenné dans le temps pondéré A est calculé au moins trois fois pour chaque configuration de l'UA. Le niveau de pression acoustique surfacique moyenné dans le temps à utiliser pour le calcul du niveau de puissance acoustique d'une configuration de l'UA est la moyenne arithmétique des deux valeurs les plus élevées dont l'écart est inférieur ou égal à 1 dB.

**Informations à publier**

Le rapport contient les données techniques nécessaires à l'identification de la source soumise à l'essai ainsi que le code d'essai et les données acoustiques. La valeur du niveau de puissance acoustique pondéré A à publier est la valeur la plus élevée des différentes configurations de l'UA testées, arrondie au nombre entier le plus proche.

**Indication du niveau de puissance acoustique garanti**

L'indication du niveau de puissance acoustique garanti doit se composer du chiffre unique correspondant à la valeur du niveau de puissance acoustique mesuré ou garanti exprimée en dB, du signe LWA et d'un pictogramme.

**Niveau de puissance acoustique maximal par classe d'UA**

Le niveau de puissance acoustique maximal par classe d'UA (y compris les périodes de transition) est indiqué dans la norme.

Voici un résumé du texte :

**Essai d'endurance pour les sources lumineuses LED et OLED**

L'essai d'endurance est réalisé pour tester la durée de vie et la performance des sources lumineuses LED et OLED.

**Conditions ambiantes et configuration d'essai**

Les cycles de commutation sont réalisés dans un local à une température ambiante de 25 ± 10 °C et une vitesse de l'air moyenne inférieure à 0,2 m/s. Les sources lumineuses sont testées à 230 V et 50 Hz.

**Méthode pour les essais d'endurance**

1. Mesure initiale du flux : mesure du flux lumineux avant le démarrage du cycle de commutation.
2. Cycles de commutation : faire fonctionner la source lumineuse pendant 1 200 cycles de commutations répétés en continu sans interruption.
3. Mesure finale du flux : noter les éventuelles défaillances de sources lumineuses et mesurer le flux lumineux des sources lumineuses qui fonctionnent.
4. Calcul du facteur de survie : diviser le flux final par le flux initial et calculer la moyenne des valeurs obtenues sur le nombre total d'unités encore en état de fonctionnement.

**Critères de référence**

Les meilleures techniques disponibles sur le marché pour les sources lumineuses et les appareillages de commande séparés sont :

* Sources lumineuses non dirigées sur tension de secteur : 120-140 lm/W
* Sources lumineuses dirigées sur tension de secteur : 90-100 lm/W
* Sources lumineuses dirigées ne fonctionnant pas sur secteur : 85-95 lm/W
* Sources lumineuses linéaires (tubes) : 140-160 lm/W
* Appareillages de commande séparés : efficacité énergétique de 95 %

**Exclusion du mercure**

Les sources lumineuses et les appareillages de commande séparés qui contiennent du mercure sont excluses.

Η καταλογοποίηση των καρτών και τις πληροφορίες που πρέπει να προσεγγιστούν για την εισαγωγή προς διαπραγμάτευση, περιλαμβάνει:

4. Χώρα ή χώρες όπου επιδιώκεται η εισαγωγή προς διαπραγμάτευση σε ρυθμιζόμενη αγορά (ή αγορές).

7. Αριθμός σειράς.
8. Αριθμός τμήματος.

Η οδηγία 2014/53/ΕΕ διατάζει την απόφαση (EU) 2014/53/EU για τον έλεγχο της πυρηνικής ενέργειας και ραδιοελεκτρονικής ασφάλειας, η οποία μετεξέχουν την εύρεση και τη διάβρωση των ραδιοηπείων. 

Οι εκτεταμένες εγκαταστάσεις που εκτελείνται στο χώρο της υψιστίας (πάνω από 10 μ.μ.) απαιτούν την εξοικείωση με τις τεχνικές απαιτήσεις της οδηγίας.

Οι εγκαταστάσεις που εκτελένονται σε εσωτερικούς σοδεισμούς και απομακρυσμένες περιοχές (πτώση έως 5 μ.μ.) απαιτούν τη συμμόρφωση με την απαίτηση για τη μετριασμό της ραδιοηπείων.

Οι ηρεμικές εγκαταστάσεις που εκτελένονται σε εσωτερικούς σοδεισμούς και απομακρυσμένες περιοχές (πτώση έως 5 μ.μ.) απαιτούν τη συμμόρφωση με την απαίτηση για τη μετριασμό της ραδιοηπείων, που είναι 40 dBm/MHz.

Οι ηρεμικές εγκαταστάσεις που εκτελένονται σε εσωτερικούς σοδεισμούς και απομακρυσμένες περιοχές (πτώση έως 5 μ.μ.) απαιτούν τη συμμόρφωση με την απαίτηση για τη μετριασμό της ραδιοηπείων, που είναι 40 dBm/MHz.

Συμπληρωτικά, οι συσκευές που εκτελένονται σε εσωτερικούς σοδεισμούς και απομακρυσμένες περιοχές (πτώση έως 5 μ.μ.) απαιτούν τη συμμόρφωση με την απαίτηση για τη μετριασμό της ραδιοηπείων, που είναι 40 dBm/MHz.

Ο προστέγοντας ορίσματος αναφέρεται σε ηρεμική κλίμακα και ονομάζεται LDC (Low-Dose Clamps), whereas ο προστέγοντας ορίσματος DAA (Device Attenuation Adjustment) αναφέρεται σε εναλλακτική κλίμακα.

Πατερά, 
Απάντηση
Συνοψίζοντας, οι κατοχούλοι λογαριασμών του ΕΤΛ πρέπει να έχουν πρόσβαση σε ολικές πληροφορίες για τους λογαριασμούς προορισμού και προέλευσης, με εκτός της αιτήσies του article 29(1) της οδηγίας 2003/87/ΕΚ.
###################################################
Αντιστοιχιστική Επιτροπή της ΕΕ
Επιτροπή της Ευρωπαϊκής Ένωσης που είναι υπεύθυνα για την ανταλλαγή και τον आदήγωμα των π nationalellern των κράτων-μέλων της ΕΕ.
###################################################
Στο πadroshmático "Αρμοστεία" και "Επικύρωση" παρέχθηκαν подробές για την αρμόδια αρχή που διοικεί την ανωτέρα αίτησης, τον πλήρη φάκελος της αίτησης και τον εκδίδομενη από την αρμόδια αρχή εξοικειωση, το πιστοποιητικό τύπου του προϊόντος, την επικύρωσή του και τη διαδικασία της έγκρισης βάσει οδηγίας τεχνικών προδιαγραφών. Σημειώνεται ότι μια αίτηση για πιστοποίηση δεν συνεπάγεται technical review και το πλήρη φάκελος της αίτησης παραληφθεί από την επικυρούσα αρχή, το πιστοποιητικό εκδίδεται εντός τριών έως πέντε εβδομάδων. 

Παρέχθηκαν επίσης πληροφορίες για τις διακρίσεις «μείζονος/ελάσσονος σημασίας», «σημαντικό/μη σημαντικό» και για την εξεταστική διαδικασία που αναφέρεται στους ανωτέρω πίνακες.
###################################################
Η αναφορά του μήνυματος BERMAN είναι αφιερωμένη στην ασφάλεια των πλοίων και των λιμενικών εγκαταστάσεων, με την οποία η Σイスουατική Εταιρεία για τη Δικαιωποίηση του Πλοίου (BERMAN) εγκρίθηκε από τον Διεθνή Οργανισμό Εμπορικής và Ναυτιλικής Ασφάλειας (ΔΝΟ), στην 14η session της Conferment of the Facilitation and Electronic Business, FAL.5/Εγκ.15, 9 Σεπτεμβρίου 2011.

Η Σイスουατική Εταιρεία για τη Δικαιωποίηση του Πλοίου (BERMAN) εγκρίθηκε από τον Διεθνή Οργανισμό Εμπορικής και Ναυτιλικής Ασφάλειας (ΔΝΟ), στην 14η session της Conferment of the Facilitation and Electronic Business, FAL.5/Εγκ.15, 9 Σεπτεμβρίου 2011.

 EU Regulatons
###################################################
Διαδικασίες δοκιμών για ηχητική πίεση επιφάνειας μετρήσεων πιέσεων σε μη-EΑ. Ο σταθμισμένος ως προς τον χρόνο μέσος όρος της Α-σταθμισένης στάθμης ηχητικής πίεσης επιφάνειας μετράται τουλάχιστον τρεις φορές για κάθε διαμόρφωση μηΕΑ. Εάν τουλάχιστον δύο από τις τιμές μέτρησης δεν διαφέρουν περισσότερο από 1 dB, δεν απαιτούνται περαιτέρω μετρήσεις. Ο σταθμισμένος ως προς τον χρόνο μέσος όρος της στάθμης ηχητικής πίεσης επιφάνειας που χρησιμοποιείται για τον υπολογισμό της στάθμης ηudioπείσης σε ορισμένη διαμόρφωση του μηΕΑ είναι ο αριθμητικός μέσος των δύο υψηλότερων τιμών που δεν διαφέρουν περισσότερο από 1 dB.

Η έκθεση περιλαμβάνει τα τεχνικά δεδομένα που είναι απαραίτητα για την ταυτοποίηση της υπό δοκιμή πηγής, καθώς και τον κώδικα δοκιμής θορύβου και τα ακουστικά δεδομένα. Η τιμή της Α-スタθμισμένης στάθμης ηχητικής ισχύος προς υποβολή είναι η υψηλότερη τιμη των διαφορετικών διαμορφωσεων του μηΕΑ που έχουν υποβληθεί σε δοκιμή, στρογγυλοποιημένη προς τον πλησιέστερο ακέρiaoariθμό.

Η ένδειξη της εγγυημένης στάθμης ηχητικής ισχύος αποτελείται από τον μοναδικό αριθμο της εγγυημένης ηudioπείσης σε dB, το σύμβολο LWA και εικονόγραμμα με την ακόλουθη μορφή.

Μερός 15: Μερική στάθμη ηχητικής ισχύος ανά κατηγορία μηΕΑ.
###################################################
Ο παρόντα κανονισμός ορίζει τις απαιτήσεις που πρέπει να εfüτχουν τα μετρούμενα μοντέλα. ΠεραίτεRON, για instance, είναι το μοντέλο που χρησιμοποιείται ως παράδειγμα. Στο σημείο 3 αναφέρεται σε την έπαλήθευση του μοντέλου και των ισοδύναμων τουςimoniomovς με τον παρόντα κανονισμό. 

Στο σημείο 4, για το ανταλλακτικά τεμάχια των modelos, αναφέρεται στην έπαλήθευση του μοντέλου. Στο σημείο 5, αναφέρεται στις απαιτήσεις για την επιτυχία της έπαλήθευσης του μοντέλου. Στό σημείο 6, αναφέρεται σε η έπαλήθευση του môντेलου. 

Στο σημείο 7, αναφέρεται στην καλοποίηση των ανοχών επαλήθευσης από τις αρχές.

Върху тема "Допускане до търговия и организиране на посредничеството" се разказва върху допусkanе до търговия на ценните книжи, организация на вторичния пазар, анализ на важните условия при това. Върху допускането до търговия, цените книжата трябва да се уведоми с оглед на разпространението на цените книжи и да се обявява, че от тях е изключенствено заявление за допускане до търговия, като се посочат най-ранните дати, на които цента книжа ще бъде допусната до търговия. Върху пазарите за растеж на МСП и МСТ, всички пазари, на които вече се смеят ценните книжи от същия клас да се предлагат или допуснати до търговия. При допускане до търговия на цента книжа, трябва да се даде подробна информация за лицата, които действат като посредници при търгуването на вторичния пазар и какъв е основният условия на техния ангажимент. Върху гарантията на цените книжи се дава информация за емисионната цена на ценните книжі.

Горният текст описва изискванията за радиочастотните услуги в България, определени от Речонестна комисия на САС при Министерство на communicacions и informations. Възможно е да се делат на 24 отделения, което представлява целият текст.

В тази дdocumentация са изложени важните изисквания за радиочастотните услуги в България, които трябваме да отговаряймо, когато са издадени във Високите цифри (V2).

Регистърът на ЕС се практикува в рамките на ЕКТП за търговия с емисии и фиксира всички важни данни относно партиди, продадени, продадени с прехвърляне или прехвърлени към Регистъра.

Регламентът е задължителен в своя цялост и се прилага пряко във всички държави членки на ЕС.

Текстът описва процесите за издаване и сертификат на типа, изделията, отнемателните работи и процедурами за прилагане в китайската регулаторна система на електронните компоненти. Серификат на тип се издава от китайския technical agent, зависейщо от промяните и ремонти на продукта, отменето на сертификата или прилагане на допълнителен сертификат. Процесите за прилагане включват заверяване с по-широки criterия, както в административния процедура, така и при промените и ремонти, които стават важни, отменето на сертификата или прилагане на допълнителен сертификат. Класификацията на промяните се извършва в категории „малка“/„значителна“, „съществена“, „несъществена“.

Горният текст е пълен код на ММО, който се използва за обмен данни между двети страни в рамките на търговия и други экономически обменки. Кодът съдържал следните важни informationsи:

1. Кодна идентификатор на элемента от данни: 3055
2. Кодна идентификатор на измерване: 6311
3. Квалификатор за прилагането на измерване: ААЕ измерване
4. Данни от измерването: „G“ Бруто тегло, с кое се measured в metric tonnes.
5. Квалификатор за измерителните единици: KGM, TNE
6. Мярка за измеримост: „UNT“, която указва, че данният е за measuring surface или layer.
7. Край и проверка на пълнотата на съобщението: 0074, „UNZ“
8. Директиви: D[USE 1] се използва при кодовете XXXXX.
9. Международни standardi:
	* компендиум от ММО относно улесняване и електронния бизнес.
	* Международен кодекс за сигурност на корабите и пристанищните съоръжения (ISPS)
10. Директива 2010/65/ЕС на Европейския парламент и Съвета от 20 октомври 2010 г.
11. Обмен данни и търговия с ММО.

Кодът отгоре е важен за обмен данни между двети страни в рамките на търговия и други ekonomически обменки, и се използва за предоставяне сведения за кораби, пристигащи във и/или напускащи пристанищата на държавите членки.
###################################################
 Regламент за ЛУС (Лисеен Управителски Сertификат).  

Анализа: 
В този документ се предоставя детайлно разъяснение за отчетите и изискванията на съответствия, както и важните сдобродения за операторите на БЛС. 

Ключови тени в тази информация са: 
- Оператора на БЛС трябва да разполага Лисеен Управителски Сertификат (LUС) за да смеши експлоатация.
- LUС включва самоличност, правата и разрешения на експлоатация на оператора на БЛС. 
- LUС се издава от компетентния орган след като се убеди, че операторът на БЛС се справи с изискванията на точки UAS.LUC.020, UAS.LUC.030 и UAS.LUC.040.
- LUС е валиден при условие, че притежателят го оставя да се разполага с него, както и при липса на оттегляне или анулиране.
- LUС се прехвърля не в случай на промяна в собствеността на организацията. 
- LUС се издава за неограничен срок и остава валиден при условие на постоянното спазване от притежателя на съответните изисквания и на държавата членка, издала удостоверението.
###################################################
Текстът се отнася до стандарт за акустично изпитване на БВС (Бroadcasting and Telecommunications Systems). В него се определят основните параметри за измерване на шума и акустичните данни, както и обозначенията на гарантираното ниво на звуковата мощност.

Включително:

*   Съответствия на изпитвания към стандарт АНСИ 7241:2006-10
*   Използване на БВС с шум
*   Изпитващо съоръжение с акустично изпитване
*   Изпитвани конфигурации на БВС
*   Технически данни за measuring noise
*   Акустични данни за измерването на шума и звуковата мощност.
*   Времевиervalsи за изпитвания и мястото за сдейбането на данните.
*   Общите характеристически данни, както и възможностите за обмен данни между БВС.

Клас BVS
Върхната част от крива А
Предполагаща място за измерване на шума
Новите измервания се извършват след това, когато:
*   Времено усреднено ниво на звуковото налягане върху измерvatelnата повърхнина е по-малко или равно на 1 dB от по-ниските ниво на звуковата мощност за дадените конфигурации на БВС.
*   Три пъти измервания се извършват върху измерvatelnата повърхнина след това, когато:
*   Времено усреднено ниво на звуковото налягане върху измервателната повърхнина е по-малко или равно на 1 dB от по-ниските ниво на звуковата мощност за дадените конфигурации на БВС.
*   Времено усреднено ниво на звуковото налягане върху измерvatelnата повърхнина се извършва поне три пъти за всяка конфигурация на БВС.
*   Двете най-високи стойности, чието отклонение е по-малко или равно на 1 dB от по-ниските ниво на звуковата мощност за дадените конфигурации на БВС са измервани върху измерvatelnата повърхнина.
*   Времено усреднено ниво на звуковото налягане върху измервателната povърхнина, което трябва да се използва за определяне на нивото на звуковата мощност за дадените конфигурации на БВС, е средноаритметично на двете най-високи стойности, чието отклонение е по-малко или равно на 1 dB от по-ниските ниво на звуковата мощност за дадените конфигурации на БВС.
*   Докладът трябва да съдържа техническите данни, необходими за идентификация на изпитвания източник, както и стандарт за измерване на шума и акустичните данни.

Текстът представява правила за класификация и класificaция на светлинни източници, които се използват в отрасли като електроника, телевизорите и други електронни Devices. Правилата включват различните типове светлинни източници, основани на нивата на комутация, както са насочени, ненасочени, линейни и други. 

Светлинните източници се класификат върху базова стойност за сравнение на екологичния аспект на светлинното отдаване, която е определена по основание на количествените показатели, например KDF % или светлинен поток на единя вълнено-целюстка (lm/W). 

Базовата стойност за сравнение се определя в зависимост от типовете на светлинните източници и от най-добрите нынешни технологии, които са достъпни на пазара. Във възможността, когато такива технологии не се могат да постигнат, базовата стойность за сравнение се определя на основание други критерия, както е приложение IV, таблица 6 от настоящия регламент.

The text provides a list of technical requirements for electronic equipment operating in specific frequency ranges within the European Union's radio spectrum. These requirements aim to protect various radio services and ensure coexistence among different users.

**Key Requirements:**

1. **Device Types:** The text defines four device types:
	* Fixed installations
	* Non-fixed installations (portable devices)
	* Outdoor installations
	* Indoor installations
2. **Frequency Ranges:** Devices are restricted to specific frequency ranges, including:
	* 3.1 GHz - 4.8 GHz
	* 8.5 GHz - 9 GHz
	* 1.215 GHz to 1.73 GHz
	* 2.5 GHz to 2.69 GHz and 2.7 GHz to 3.4 GHz
3. **Power Limitations:**
	* Maximum mean e.i.r.p. (Electromagnetic Irradiance Power Density) spectral density:
		+ 3.1 GHz - 4.8 GHz band: –41.3 dBm/MHz
		+ Other bands: varies depending on frequency range
	* Peak e.i.r.p.: depends on frequency range and band
	* LBT (Listen Before Talk): maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density:
		+ 1.215 GHz to 1.73 GHz: –70 dBm/MHz
		+ 2.5 GHz to 2.69 GHz and 2.7 GHz to 3.4 GHz: –50 dBm/MHz
4. **Duty Cycle:** Limitation of duty cycle to 10% per second.
5. **Fixed Outdoor Installations:** Not permitted.
6. **Radio Astronomy Service (RAS):** Total power spectral density must be below –65 dBm/MHz in specific frequency ranges.

**Mitigation Techniques:**

1. DAA (Device-Assisted Architecture) mitigation technique:
	* Allowed for devices in 3.1 GHz - 4.8 GHz and 8.5 GHz - 9 GHz bands
	* Maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of –41.3 dBm/MHz
2. LBT mechanism:
	* Allowed for devices in specific frequency ranges
	* Maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density varies depending on frequency range

**Alternative Mitigation Techniques:**

Devices may use alternative mitigation techniques if they ensure at least equivalent performance and level of spectrum protection to comply with Directive 2014/53/EU and technical requirements of this Decision.

Note that some specific details, such as the exact definitions of e.i.r.p. and LBT mechanisms, are not provided in the text and would require additional resources or expert knowledge to fully understand.

The EU Emissions Trading System (EU ETS) is a regulatory framework that aims to reduce greenhouse gas emissions in Europe. The EU ETS consists of several components, including:

1. **Union Registry**: A database that stores information on allowances and Kyoto units.
2. **EUTL (European Union ETS Tracking Platform)**: A website that provides information on the EU ETS, including:
	* National allocation tables
	* Aviation allocation tables
	* Total number of allowances held in the Union Registry
	* Fees charged by national administrators
3. **Public Website**: The EUTL's public website displays general information about the EU ETS, including:
	* Sum of verified emissions by Member State (as a percentage)
	* Percentage share belonging to accounts administered by a particular Member State in allowance and Kyoto unit transfer transactions
4. **Completed Transaction Records**: Information on completed transactions is displayed on the public website, including:
	* Account holder name and account identifier
	* Amount of allowances or Kyoto units involved
	* Transaction identification code
	* Date and time at which the transaction was completed
5. **Agreements in Force**: Information on agreements that are in force pursuant to Directive 2003/87/EC is published on the public website, including:
	* Holdings of allowances issued in linked emissions trading systems
	* Number of allowances issued for compliance in EU ETS

**Important Dates:**

* 30 April (Krticle) marks important deadlines for reporting and submitting information.

**Account Holder Information:**

* The Union Registry's website provides real-time access to account holder information, including:
	+ Current holdings of allowances and Kyoto units
	+ List of proposed transactions initiated by the account holder
	+ Completed transactions, including transaction details and response codes.

The text is a regulation regarding the Innovation Fund, a funding scheme for projects related to innovation and research. The key points are:

**Innovation Fund Regulation**

* The regulation outlines the rules for carrying out audits on financial statements and reports of Union contributions.
* Audits must be conducted by independent auditors using internationally accepted audit standards to provide reasonable assurance.
* The report of the auditor and related documentation must be made available upon request to the European Parliament, Commission, Court of Auditors, and Member State authorities.

**Communication, Knowledge Sharing, and Publicity**

* Project proponents must proactively make publicly available information on their websites about projects supported under this regulation.
* This information should include an explicit reference to the Innovation Fund support received.
* The project proponents must also ensure that information is provided in a coherent, effective, and targeted manner.

**Final Provisions**

* The regulation will enter into force 20 days after its publication in the Official Journal of the European Union.
* It will be binding in its entirety and directly applicable in all Member States.
* Specific seminars, workshops, or other activities will be organized to facilitate exchanges of experience, knowledge, and best practices.

Overall, the regulation aims to ensure transparency, accountability, and effective communication about Innovation Fund projects.

The text outlines the requirements for a UAS (Unmanned Aircraft Systems) License to Fly (LUC) holder, which is an operator who conducts civil UAS operations.

**Key Requirements:**

1. **Safety Management System**: The LUC holder must have a safety management system in place, which includes procedures such as:
	* Safety reporting and internal investigations
	* Operational control
	* Communication on safety
	* Training and safety promotion
	* Compliance monitoring
	* Safety risk management
	* Management of change
2. **Documentation**: The LUC holder must maintain documentation, including an LUC manual that describes the organization's procedures, activities, and personnel.
3. **Certification and Approval**: The competent authority (the body responsible for issuing the LUC) will issue a license after verifying compliance with relevant requirements.

**Important Provisions:**

1. **Privileges of the LUC holder**: The competent authority may grant privileges to the LUC holder, including the ability to authorize operations without submitting an operational declaration or applying for an operational authorization.
2. **Changes in the LUC management system**: Any changes requiring approval by the competent authority include significant changes to the safety management system and terms of approval.
3. **Transferability of the LUC**: The LUC is not transferable, except in cases where ownership is transferred with prior approval from the competent authority.

**Compliance Requirements:**

1. **Independent function for monitoring compliance**: The LUC holder must have a function to monitor the compliance and adequacy of their safety management system.
2. **Assessment and mitigation of risks inherent to subcontractors**: The LUC holder must assess and mitigate risks associated with subcontractors under their safety management system.

**Duration and Validity:**

1. **LUC shall be issued for an unlimited duration**: It remains valid as long as the LUC holder complies with relevant requirements.
2. **Revocation or surrender of an LUC**: The LUC holder must notify the competent authority without delay upon revoking or surrendering their license.

**Access and Transparency:**

1. **Granting access to personnel**: The LUC holder must grant authorized individuals access to facilities, UAS systems, documents, records, data, procedures, and other relevant materials for the purpose of demonstrating compliance with this Regulation.

Here's a summary of the noise test code:

**Objective:** Determine the A-weighted sound power levels of different types of Unmanned Aircraft (UA) classes.

**Methods:**

1. **Basic Noise Emission Standard**: Use EN ISO 3744:2010 standards.
2. **Test Setup**:
	* UA hovering above a reflecting plane (hard surface).
	* UA mounted at a safe distance from walls and ceilings.
	* Enclosed in a hemispherical measurement sphere with microphones defined by Annex F of EN ISO 3744:2010.
3. **Operating Conditions**: 
	* Test with the battery fully charged.
	* Test in stable position, laterally and vertically, 0.5 m above the measurement hemisphere.
	* If accessories are available, test with and without them.

**Calculation of Surface Time-Averaged Sound Pressure Level:**

1. Take at least three measurements for each UA configuration.
2. Use the highest values that differ by no more than 1 dB.
3. Calculate the mean value of these two highest values.

**Reporting Requirements:**

1. Technical data to identify the source under test.
2. Noise test code and acoustical data.
3. Report the A-weighted sound power level value, rounded to the nearest whole number (less than 0.5, round down; greater than or equal to 0.5, round up).

**Indication of Guaranteed Sound Power Level:**

1. Indicate the maximum sound power level in dB, with a pictogram.
2. Use a red color for the indication, and adjust size according to equipment size.

**Maximum Sound Power Levels per UA Class (including transition periods):**

| UA Class | MTOM mass (m) | Maximum Sound Power Level LWA (dB) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| C1 | 250 ≤ m < 900 | 85 |
| C2 | 900 ≤ m < 4000 | 83-81 |

Note: These values apply as from entry into force, with adjustments for periods after 2 or 4 years.
###################################################
Here is a summary of the text:

**Verification Procedure for Market Surveillance**

* The verification tolerances set out in this Annex relate only to Member State authorities and shall not be used by suppliers as an allowed tolerance.
* Values on labels or product fiche shall not be more favorable for suppliers than values reported in technical documentation.

**Non-Compliance**

* If a model is designed to detect testing conditions and automatically alter its performance, it shall be considered non-compliant.
* When verifying compliance with this Regulation, Member State authorities shall follow the following procedure:

1. Test one single unit of the model
2. Check if:
	* Declared values are not more favorable for suppliers than test reports (a)
	* Values on labels and product information sheets are not more favorable for suppliers than declared values (b)
	* Determined values comply with verification tolerances as given in Table 12 (c)
3. If results in points 2(a) and (b) are not achieved, the model and all equivalent models shall be considered non-compliant.
4. If result in point 2(c) is not achieved, select three additional units for testing
5. Model shall be considered compliant if arithmetical mean of determined values complies with verification tolerances as given in Table 12.
6. If results in point 5 are not achieved, model and all equivalent models shall be considered non-compliant.

**Verification Tolerances**

* Table 12 sets out the verification tolerances for measured parameters:
	+ Net volume: -3% or 1L lower
	+ Gross volume: -3% or 1L lower
	+ TDA (Thermal Energy Density): -3%
	+ Edaily (Energy consumption in daily operation): +10%
	+ AE (Annual energy consumption): +10%

**Other Requirements**

* Member State authorities shall use measurement and calculation methods set out in Annex IV.
* No other tolerances, such as those set out in harmonized standards or other measurement methods, shall be applied.

Here's a summary of the text:

**Light Source Regulation**

* The regulation defines a light source as a product that emits light through one or more lamps or LEDs.
* Light sources must meet certain requirements, including:
	+ Luminous flux: must be greater than 10 lm/W
	+ Chromaticity coordinates (x and y): must not deviate from the declared value by more than 10%
	+ Correlated colour temperature: must not deviate from the declared value by more than 10%
* Light sources that allow manual or automatic control of luminous intensity, color, correlated color temperature, spectrum, and/or beam angle must be tested using reference control settings.

**Endurance Testing**

* LED and OLED light sources must undergo endurance testing to verify their lumen maintenance and survival factor.
* The test involves switching cycles in a controlled environment with specific conditions (temperature, air velocity, and voltage).
* The test measures the luminous flux of the light source before and after 1,200 switching cycles.

**Benchmarking**

* The best available technology on the market for light sources has the following characteristics:
	+ Mains voltage non-directional light sources: 120-140 lm/W
	+ Mains voltage directional light sources: 90-100 lm/W
	+ Directional light sources not operating on the mains: 80-99 lm/W
	+ Linear light sources (tubes): 140-160 lm/W
* The best available technology for separate control gears has an energy efficiency of 9%.
* Features like high color rendering might prevent products from achieving these benchmarks.

**Mercury Content**

* The regulation does not have mercury content in the best available technology on the market for light sources and separate control gears.

The text outlines the technical requirements for devices operating in the a1 GHz - 4,8 GHz and 8,5 GHz - 9 GHz bands as per Directive 2014/5a/EU. The key points include:

* Devices using DAA (Device Association Agreement) mitigation technique are permitted to operate with:
	+ Maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of –41 dBm/MHz in the a1 GHz - 4,8 GHz band
	+ Maximum peak e.i.r.p. of 0 dBm defined in 50 MHz in both bands
* Devices using LBT (Listen Before Talk) mechanism are permitted to operate with:
	+ Maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of –70 dBm/MHz in the 1,215 GHz - 1,700 GHz band
	+ Maximum mean e.i.r.p. spectral density of –50 dBm/MHz and maximum peak e.i.r.p. of –10 dBm/50 MHz in the 2,500 GHz - 2,690 GHz and 2,700 GHz - a4 GHz bands respectively
* Non-fixed installations must fulfill specific requirements to protect radio services:
	+ Total power spectral density must be 10 dB below maximum e.i.r.p. spectral density in the 2,500 GHz - 2,690 GHz and 4,800 GHz - 5,000 GHz bands
	+ Total power spectral density must be 5 dB below maximum e.i.r.p. spectral density in the a4 GHz - a8 GHz band
* Devices must also comply with:
	+ Limitation of duty cycle to 10% per second
	+ No fixed outdoor installations are permitted
* Alternative mitigation techniques may be used if they ensure at least an equivalent performance and level of spectrum protection.

Note: When LDC or DAA is implemented, note 5 applies.

**Regulation on the Innovation Fund**

The Regulation establishes an innovation fund to support project development assistance projects in the European Union.

**Main Provisions**

1. **Financial Support**: The Regulation provides financial support for project development assistance projects, with a total budget of €2 billion for 2020-2027.
2. **Independence and Competence**: An independent auditor will conduct an audit on the financial statements and reports to provide reasonable assurance.
3. **Communication and Knowledge Sharing**: Project proponents must make publicly available information about their projects, including the Innovation Fund support received.

**Implementation Provisions**

1. **Timeline**: The Regulation will enter into force on the 20th day following its publication in the Official Journal of the European Union.
2. **Direct Applicability**: The Regulation is binding and directly applicable in all Member States.

**Final Provisions**

1. **Institutional Arrangements**: The Commission, the Court of Auditors, and the audit authorities of Member States will be involved in the implementation of the Regulation.
2. **International Cooperation**: International cooperation on climate change mitigation and adaptation will be facilitated through the Innovation Fund.

Overall, the Regulation aims to support innovation and entrepreneurship in the EU while promoting sustainable development and addressing climate change.

* Support for each other's technical support, data, and information exchange is allowed.

* Acceptance/Validation comments:
	+ Type certificate: automatic acceptance for some data (e.g., aircraft flight manual, engine installation manual).
	+ Supplemental type certificate: validation in accordance with Level of Involvement principles and Technical Implementation Procedures; significant changes may be validated under a streamlined process.
	+ Non-significant changes and repairs: automatic acceptance.
* Implementations:
	+ Administrative processes do not require technical investigation.
	+ Minor/major and significant/non-significant classifications are made by the Certificating Authority according to specific criteria and definitions.
	+ Changes meeting certain criteria (e.g., general configuration, assumptions used for certification) are automatically considered significant.

Overall, the text establishes a framework for cooperation between the EU and China in airworthiness oversight activities, allowing for the acceptance and validation of certificates issued within one Party's regulatory system.

The text outlines the requirements and regulations for Unmanned Aircraft Systems (UAS) operators, specifically those holding an Operator's Certificate (LUC). The key points include:

**Safety Management System**

* UAS operators must have a safety management system in place to ensure safe operations.
* The system should be integrated with other relevant certificates, such as Organization Certificates.

**Certification and Authorization**

* LUC holders must provide a manual describing their organization, procedures, and activities.
* The manual must be signed by the accountable manager confirming compliance with regulations.
* Copies of amendments must be provided to the competent authority.

**Terms of Approval**

* The competent authority issues an LUC after verifying compliance with relevant requirements.
* The LUC includes information on the UAS operator's identity, privileges, authorized operations, and any special limitations or conditions.

**Privileges and Access**

* The LUC holder is granted privileges to authorise operations without submitting operational declarations or applying for authorizations.
* The LUC holder must grant access to facilities, UAS, documents, records, data, procedures, or materials relevant to their activity to authorized persons.

**Changes and Transferrability**

* Changes to the LUC management system require prior approval from the competent authority.
* An LUC is not transferable except in cases of organizational change approved by the competent authority.

**Duration and Validity**

* An LUC is issued for an unlimited duration, valid as long as the UAS operator complies with regulations and does not surrender or revoke it.
* Upon revocation or surrender, the UAS operator must provide a digital acknowledgment to the competent authority within a specified timeframe.

The text describes a verification procedure for market surveillance purposes related to energy efficiency standards in the EU. Here's a summary:

**Verification Tolerances**: The verification tolerances set out in Table 12 relate only to Member State authorities and shall not be used by suppliers as an allowed tolerance.

**Testing Procedure**:

1. One single unit of the model is tested.
2. The model complies with the requirements if:
	* Declared values are not more favorable for the supplier than test reports.
	* Values on the label and product information sheet are not more favorable for the supplier.
	* Energy efficiency class is not more favorable for the supplier than the declared value.
3. If results in 2(a) and (b) are not achieved, the model and all equivalent models shall be considered non-compliant.

**Additional Testing**: If the result in 2(c) is not achieved, three additional units of the same model or one or more equivalent models are selected for testing.
4. The model complies with requirements if the arithmetic mean of determined values complies with the respective tolerances given in Table 12.
5. If results in 4 are not achieved, the model and all equivalent models shall be considered non-compliant.

**Requirements**: Member State authorities must:

* Use measurement and calculation methods set out in Annex IV
* Only apply verification tolerances set out in Table 12
* Only use the procedure described for requirements referred to in this Annex

**Table 12: Verification Tolerances**

| Parameters | Verification Tolerances |
| --- | --- |
| Net volume, and net compartment volume where applicable | The determined value shall not be more than 3 or 1 L lower — whichever is the greater value — than the declared value. |
| Gross volume, and gross compartment volume where applicable | The determined value shall not be more than 3 or 1 L lower — whichever is the greater value — than the declared value. |
| TDA, and compartment TDA where applicable | The determined value shall not be more than 3 L lower than the declared value. |
| Energy efficiency class | The determined value shall not be more than 10% higher than the declared value. |
| AE | The determined value shall not be more than 10% higher than the declared value. |

Note: In cases where three additional units are tested, the determined value means the arithmetic mean of values determined for these units.

This Regulation outlines the technical requirements for light sources, including LED and OLED devices. The key points are:

**Definition of a Light Source**

* A light source is defined as an article that emits visible light through incandescence or electroluminescence.
* Its characteristics include:
	+ Luminous flux (lm)
	+ Chromaticity coordinates (x and y)
	+ Correlated colour temperature (K)
	+ Colour rendering index
	+ Spectral distribution

**Technical Requirements**

* Light sources must meet specific limits for each of the above characteristics, with a tolerance of 10% except for correlated colour temperature.
* Linear LED or OLED light sources must undergo endurance testing to verify their luminous flux maintenance and survival factor.

**Endurance Testing**

* The test consists of 1,200 cycles of repeated, continuous switching on/off without interruption.
* Each cycle consists of 150 minutes of the light source switched ON followed by 30 minutes of it switched OFF.
* The total test time is 3,600 hours.
* The lumen maintenance factor (XLMF) must be at least 90%.

**Best Available Technology**

* Mains voltage non-directional light sources: 120-140 lm/W
* Mains voltage directional light sources: 90-100 lm/W
* Directional light sources not operating on the mains: 85-95 lm/W
* Linear light sources (tubes): 140-160 lm/W

**Separate Control Gears**

* The best available technology for separate control gears has an energy efficiency of 95%.

Note that this summary is a condensed version of the original text, and some details may have been omitted to maintain clarity.

    *   Datum und Uhrzeit des Abschlusses der Transaktion (mitteleuropäische Zeit)
    *   Transaktionstyp

Die Registrierung ist wichtig, um die Transparenz und Rechenschaftspflicht im EU-Emissionshandelssystem zu gewährleisten.
